So whenever you let go of an attachment, just say, I'm just not going to be focused on that anymore, you free up your attention. Attention is a facet of consciousness and then your attention can go somewhere else. You'll find the experience very liberating, and after all, we're at the top of the liberating current now. So something I want to bring here as we talk about the seventh chakra and the expansion of consciousness is the power of Kundalini. Kundalini is a very powerful force. It's concentrated prana or Shakti or charge. Shakti is the goddess of energy in the Hindu cosmology. And Kundalini is such highly-concentrated charge that it is said to be a like a hot poker that pokes through the knots in a stick of bamboo. Well, we have knots in our chakras. In Sanskrit, they're called Granthis and they are knots that keep the energy from passing through. And I think of them often as where we are not or where we cannot or where we will not instead of just K-N-O-T, the knots that tie us up. But Kundalini is a powerful force. The name really refers to Kundala which means coiled and her full name is Kundalini Shakti, a form of the goddess that takes this concentrated energy and rises chakra by chakra up the spine, piercing each chakra in turn and rising up to the crown. And one reason they call it Kundalini and name it after the form of a serpent, is sometimes when people have Kundalini awakening, they vibrate and they tremble and they move in a kind of serpentine wave-like fashion. So Kundalini is a powerful healing and awakening force but it's a very tricky and unpredictable force to play with. Many people say that the only way to receive Kundalini is through grace. We can invite it through our meditations and our yoga and our practices, but it doesn't happen for everybody and it happens to some people without doing any of that. So we can invite it but we can't control it. Many people say you get it from contact with a guru who awakens these energies within you and that it's only safe to practice Kundalini under the teaching of a guru who is educated and capable in these matters. But I mentioned it here because many people get spontaneous Kundalini awakenings and when that happens, they often don't know quite what's going on or how to tolerate it or how to handle it or treat it. And so if it happens to you, know that it's a powerful healing force that is trying to break through your blocks and take you back to wholeness. You might experience visions, you might hear voices, you might feel tingling or movement in your body, it might keep you awake at night. If that Kundalini awakening is difficult for you and many people have come to me over the years with difficulties with this, I usually find that it's lack of ground, that the energy is only moving up and that's moving toward freedom, yes, but if we have too much freedom, it can become chaos and we need to ground and anchor down into the body. You may need to eat something, you may need to have somebody hug you or touch you to help bring the energy back down to your lower chakras that usually kind of smooths out the difficulty of this ride. But if you can open to it, it's a great healer and awakener. The objective of this quest is not necessarily to awaken your Kundalini. What it is is to open and clear your chakras so that if Kundalini should awaken, there's fewer blocks to push through and you can enjoy and tolerate that spiritual energy. So in this chakra, we want to develop our higher mind. We want to develop and go to higher consciousness, our higher power. And as we release attachment, we find that we're more letting go, we're going in to surrender. Most people that have a spiritual awakening describe it as a kind of interior surrender, a surrender to something greater, a surrender to grace. So think of a difficulty in your life. Take it into meditation. Tune in to a greater field of wisdom. Form the question in your mind. A question is like a browser on your computer. When you type that in, it goes out in this vast field of information that we know is the internet and it downloads the websites that might bring you that answer. So when you ask a question in your mind, you are calling in that information. Sit quietly and just surrender to what comes. Take it dispassionately. Don't decide if it's true or not or good or bad. Just watch. Be it your silent witness. Let that information come to you and it may come in that moment, it may come a few days later, it might come in a dream or a chance conversation with a friend, but the more you put out that question, the more you invite the information to come in. I've sat with a question sometimes for six months or a year. When I wrote Waking The Global Heart, I asked the question, what's the next organizing principle for humanity? And books would tumble into my lap and conversations would happen that would contribute to that until finally, I felt like I had my answer. So if you're struggling with the question of where do you go in your life, what to do about a relationship or a health problem or where to live or career, let yourself sit with a question and don't expect an answer right away. Sometimes, we have to gather a lot of information before the answer comes. Be willing to sit in the unknowing because if you get the answer too soon, there's a whole lot that you're going to miss. So open your mind and see what comes. Know the divine mind always has a plan for your best growth. So your exercise for today is to practice this. Ask a question that you want guidance on. Sit in meditation and notice what happens in your mind, in your conversations, in your dreams, write it in your journal, share it with the tribe, and see what happens. Start incorporating that higher mind. For your seventh chakra skillset, I encourage you to enter into meditation, to practice being in the silent witness. Remember we asked who's living in there? Just sit and ask that question. Who is it that's thinking these thoughts? Who is it that is feeling what I'm feeling? Who is it that's asking this question? How do I know? And just practice observing yourself dispassionately without judgment, without changing anything, just be in your silent witness so that it concludes the first part of chakra seven. So tomorrow would be our day of going into the body but the seventh chakra doesn't have a whole lot to do with the body. So instead, we're going to go into a deep meditation, the primary practice for this chakra. Can't wait to share that with you. In the meantime, write down your reflections and breakthroughs and share it with the tribe. See you tomorrow!

LESSON 23 - Crown Chakra: Expanding Awareness
--------------------
<v ->Welcome back to what would be our body day,</v> but instead we're going into a meditation since the seventh chakra is more about consciousness than the body. Not that the body's void of consciousness by any means, as you will see in this meditation. So find a comfortable place to sit where you can be upright, your crown placed above your base. Tuck your tailbone to the back, draw into your core, and lift your crown up to the heavens while keeping your roots down. Close your eyes, and withdraw your attention from the outer world. And come into the deep and infinite inner world of your own awareness. Let go of everything outside of you and embrace the divine being that lives within your body. Open to your breath. Open to your breath, and notice what it feels like when your body fills with air. And what it's like to release the air. Feel yourself as the breath, inhaling and exhaling, expanding and contracting. Notice the awareness that can become aware of your breath. Notice that that awareness can be directed in the form of attention to anything you choose. And we're going to first direct our awareness to our body. Take an internal scan of your body. Your location in the room, the way you're sitting, the clothes upon your body, the temperature on your skin. Allow yourself to be aware of any aches or pains or tensions and any pleasures that you feel in the body. As you allow your body to become still. And as you become still, you become anchored into the ground. But who is it that lives in this body? Know that you are something more than just the body. Release for a moment your physical identity and allow yourself to move deeper. Release yourself from your physical identity and allow yourself to move deeper. Now let your awareness scan your emotions. What are you feeling in this moment? Are you feeling restless or patient? Happy or sad? I hear it. Simply let your awareness scan your emotional state, even if you're not feeling any particular emotion at all, just notice that. And then ask yourself: who is it that's feeling these emotions? Know that you are more than just your feelings. Allow yourself to release your emotional identity and move deeper. Now we come up to the third chakra. Everything you do, your ego identity, who is it that you think you are in the world? Are you a singer, a mother, a teacher? A worker? A caretaker? And what are the things you do to fulfill that role? Who is it that is doing all those things? Allow yourself in this moment to let go of the urge to do anything at all. And rest in the stillness. Let go of that ego identity and know that you're something more than what you do. Release, and go deeper. Think about all the things, and people, and places that you love. And what it feels like to open your heart and really love. Breathe into your heart chakra. Let your awareness feel that love radiating out from your heart. But who's in there, who is it that is doing that loving? Who is it that connects with other people in caring and compassion? Who is it that wants to be loved? Know that this is part of who you are but there is even more. There's something behind all of that. Let go of your identity as a lover, and go deeper. Bring your awareness up to your throat chakra. Your creative expression, all the things you say, and underneath that, all the things you're trying to say. Who is that in there? That wants to say these things? Who is that that listens to the words of others? That listens to music, rhythm? Who is it that hears and speaks? Know that this is something beyond your creative identity. So release that and move deeper. Now we come to chakra six, the place of seeing. All the things you see in a day, in a week, in a year, in a lifetime. All of the things you remember and imagine. What is doing all that? Who is seeing out through your eyes? Who is imagining and remembering? And with what? Let go of the need to see, and draw your attention inward, and take one more step. Bring yourself up to consciousness itself. Who is the one that lives inside here, thinking my thoughts? Who's the one operating this vehicle, taking me on the journey? What is this faculty of consciousness that even allows me to ask this question? What is questioning? Allow yourself to be aware of your own awareness. Feel the infinity of awareness looking at itself. And then finally, imagine that there is a greater awareness that is looking at you. A greater awareness, that divine mind. A universal intelligence. A greater wisdom that is aware of you and your consciousness. And you are aware of this greater consciousness as well. And as you prepare to conclude this meditation, draw that greater awareness around you like the thousand petals of the lotus that is the symbol of the Sahasrara crown chakra. Imagine that awareness is holding you the way a mother holds a child, the way a flowerpot holds roots around the earth. That awareness is guiding you, is understanding you, is loving you, and is always there around you. Imagine those thousand petals unfold all around you and hold you in a loving embrace. And as it does, your awareness remains in the exact center of that lotus. The center of your crown chakra. And as you come out of the meditation, increase the depth of your breath. And you wiggle your fingers and toes. And at first, just open your eyes just a little tiny slit so the barest amount of light is coming through. And you feel the awareness within you, and the awareness of what's around you beginning to connect. And as you open your eyes wider and return to the world, stay centered in the middle of your thousand petal lotus even as the blossoms unfold in everything around you. Thou art that, namaste. So your exercise for today is to practice the meditation or any kind of meditation that you do. To look in your workbook to remind yourself of the challenge for this week. And make sure you share your experience and lessons with the tribe. And tomorrow we will be exploring the spirit of the crown chakra, and the path to the divine.

LESSON 24 - Crown Chakra: Healing the Spirit by Remembering Your Divine Nature
--------------------
<v ->When I look at evolution,</v> I see that evolution is the god's way of making more gods. What do I mean by that? Well, life on Earth began as single-celled organisms that spread across the planet. It took about three billion years for them to begin to put themselves together. And then we had our first multicellular creatures that became more and more complex, more and more intelligent, more and more capable, and growing into perhaps the most recent but not the last iteration of humans now walking around the planet, texting on cellphones. So as we have evolved, we have become more sophisticated, more powerful, and as I say, more intelligent. If you take this trajectory and you keep on going to total power, omnipotence, to total consciousness, omniscience, to total presence, omnipresence, you're taking a journey to the divine. As we evolve, we are becoming more like gods. We have the power to blow ourselves up, we have the power to change the climate, we have the power to influence the gene pool. For better or worse, for creation or destruction. We have the power on the scale that used to be attributed to gods. In that way, evolution is the god's way of making more gods. But are we godlike? Are we goddess-like? Well, that depends on our consciousness. Do we have the partnership with divine consciousness that enables us to hold these powers with wisdom, with balance? I think the journey through the chakras is the journey through the sacred elements, the sacred earth that brings us our base. The sacredness of pleasure, sacred, well-balanced power, sacred love or divine love, truth, beauty, and wisdom. When we partner with these divine attributes of the chakras, we are evolving our own being and we are evolving to partnership with the divine and its infinite wisdom. Many people think there's nothing beyond us. We are it. That we're not part of divinity, that there's not anything out there that we don't know anything, we can't trust our wisdom. But if you look at the universe with its trillions of galaxies, billions of stars in each one, when you look at the perfection of this planet holding its temperature, its level of oxygen, with its oceans and all the ecosystems that go together, despite what humans are doing to disrupt it, you can't deny there is a divine intelligence at work. Things are not running into entropy, there is an order in everything. So as we contemplate the divine and say what is it, what is this force of grace, of intelligence, of creation that we are privileged to witness and grow toward? And like a plant with its roots in the ground, we reach up and drink in wisdom and grace. And as we do that, we are connecting with the divine. We are taking the journey to awaken the divine within ourselves to see it within each other. So in many fairy tales, there is a story about a king and a queen. And maybe the queen gets pregnant and has a baby that maybe she isn't supposed to have, maybe there's too many kids vying for the throne already. For whatever reason, they decide they're going to let this baby go. They're going to put it in a basket and send it down the river. They're going to put it out in the woods, they're going to put it on a mountain top and make that sacrifice. And we assume if they do that, the baby might die. But we know from all these fairy tales that the baby doesn't die, that the baby in the river is found and raised by a fisherman. The baby that's left in the woods or on a hillside is found and raised by a farmer or a baker or a woodcutter. And that baby is raised with love in the world of the common people. It's raised to know their ways, it's raised to be grounded in the practical ways of life, and it's raised with love, but perhaps with parents that have some limitations. And it follows in these fairy tales that sometime around the point of late adolescents, as the child is becoming an adult, through a series of adventures or through a quest or through coincidences, they find their way back to the kingdom and they discover who their parents really are, not the mortal common people that raised them, but the king and the queen. And that they're really set to inherit the throne and become a prince or a princess or a king and a queen themselves. Well to me, this is a metaphor for the mortal parents that raised us with love and did the best they could and taught us the ways of the world that we needed to learn to remember our connection with the commonality of all humanity. And yet, our real parents are the divine mother and the divine father, the goddess and the god in whatever or the myriad forms that they take, a feminine form of divinity, a masculine form of divinity, and that we ourselves are what in mythology is called the divine child. The divine child is said to have powers that are beyond either of its parents. The divine child is said to bring something to the world that has never existed before through understanding who they really are, that each of us is a divine spark, a son or a daughter of the divine mother and father working in partnership. So we are here to experience divine consciousness, to experience the creation of a miracle, and to see life itself and everything that happens as a miracle. It's a miracle that you just turned on your tap and water comes out that you can drink. It's a miracle that a baby comes out of the womb fully formed. It's a miracle that we meet the partner in life, that we find our way, that everything in the city happens, the garbage gets taken out and the food gets taken in and people have jobs, most of them, and that we somehow get along together in a divine order. If you're going to learn to create miracles, first you have to see them. You have to see that the divine is in everything. It's shining with a sparkling luster. It is truth, consciousness, and bliss. It is behind the sacred order and that we are sacred beings embedded in a sacred universe, and our job is to awaken that, to see it, to live it, to be it, and to harness divine consciousness and bring it down through our chakras to shine out into the world. That is the true meaning of namaste. Namaste means the divine lives in me in an awakened state and the divine lives in you and the divine is in everything around me. Namaste. So when we forget that the divine is in everything, and we treat matter as just some substance that we can do whatever we want to with, we treat other people as if they didn't matter, and we create many crises in our world. You could see this in some way that we have moved away from the sacred, we have moved away from the divine, and in that, nothing matters, nothing means anything, nothing's worth anything. It's all dispensable and we begin destroying it. So if we want to change this paradigm, we have to start with treating ourselves as sacred, treating the ground we walk on as sacred, the food we eat, the people we know and interact with everyday as sacred, divine beings that we are here together to create heaven on Earth, to learn how to create a miracle, and we change ourselves from the inside by remembering that we are a god or a goddess walking this Earth to bring blessings. For the next 24 hours, and make it a practice that perhaps you do everyday, see the divinity in everything. Treat each object as if it were sacred. Even if you throw away a piece of paper, say thank you for the time that you used it. Thank you to the tree that gave its birth. If you eat, say thank you for what you're eating. If you have an interaction with a friend, say thank you. Realize that the universe is here to shower you with divine blessings if you can just open to receive it. The divine gave us life. The only thing it asks in return is that we give our gifts back. So take a deep breath, congratulations! We have concluded the upward liberating current moving all the way from the first chakra up to the crown. If you've gotten this far, really pat yourself on the back. Give yourself a hug. Say a real to the tribe. You've taken quite a quest and quite a journey. From here, we're going to examine where we've gotten to and then we're going to start the journey back down, taking our divine consciousness down through vision, through communication, through relationship, through empowerment and action, through moving with passion into life and through manifesting our highest aspirations and our true purpose. So fasten your seat belts 'cause that's going to be a fast ride down. It's going to be lots of fun. We're going to change the format and you're going to learn exercises to do with another person. It's great for coaches, great for finding your way. We're going to laugh and we're going to enjoy. We're going to create the world that we know in our hearts is possible.

LESSON 26 - Begin Your Downward Manifesting Current
--------------------
<v ->Welcome back.</v> And once again, congratulations for completing the upward current for all the work you've done to get here, for sticking through this quest and continuing to hunt for the treasure. Now we're going to begin our descent so fasten your seat belts, just like when you're in a plane and the captain says we're getting ready to go in for a landing. You got to put your tray table up. Fasten your seat belts 'cause we're going to take a rapid descent down to the earth to learn how to bring heaven down to earth, to learn how to manifest your highest aspirations. So in the journey upward, you did a lot of healing on yourself. You learned the movements, you practiced the yoga, you were clearing your chakras and you were taking the steps to go up to higher awareness. But the question is in this spiritual journey, what do we then do with that higher awareness? Now, comes the time to make it practical, to learn how to apply it to your life, to create the life you want, the life of your dreams. So why is it important to work on both channels? The upward current of liberation takes us from our fixed forms. We go from earth to water, water's a little freer than the fixed earth. To fire that's radiating upward, to air that's invisible, to sound, to light and to consciousness getting freer and freer with each step. In the downward current, we are taking our higher consciousness and bringing it into a vision. We're talking about it, we're bringing it into our relationships, we're doing something about it. We're bringing things together and moving things into place and we're manifesting our dream. Both currents are always working together in the chakra system. We're taking energy in from our thoughts, from consciousness, from the divine, from grace. We're bringing it down and we're always evolving and moving out of limitations and expanding and moving up. And the two currents passing each other create a vortex, the wheeling, spinning disk that we describe as the chakras, as remember the word means wheel or disk. And so, these are always working together, they're always mixing together. When you're in your lower chakras, you have only a little bit of the liberating current and a lot of the manifesting current. So you have things that you can feel and see and touch. When you're in the higher chakras you have more of the liberating current but not so much of the manifesting current, so things might be a little vague and ethereal. But as we go down we get denser and denser and more specific with each step. Now, what's very natural to feel when you go on the downward current is resistance. Because when you go from a plane of less density to a plane of more density, you experience a little resistance. Think of a meteor that's coming in from outer space, it's going through the vacuum of outer space and it has no resistance. And then as it comes toward the earth, you feel it hit the atmosphere. The atmosphere gives just a little bit of resistance then it goes through the atmosphere, might catch fire and then it hits the ocean. Well, the ocean is thicker than the atmosphere so it experiences even more resistance. Until finally maybe it goes all the way to the bottom of the ocean and it hits land, that's the ultimate resistance, it can't go any farther. So when we go from thought planes to trying to be specific about what we're imagining or we take it out of our imagination and we try to tell somebody what we're talking about, that requires being more specific. When we try to bring it in to our relationships, everything requires getting a little more clear, a little more concrete, a little more formed, and into a little less freedom. So it's natural to feel resistance. And what we experience in that resistance is more blockages in the chakras and what we're going to learn in this downward current is some methods to clear out those resistances so that you are straight on course from your highest thought all the way down to what you manifest. And we'll learn that chakra by chakra. So, let's apply these principles to something like building a house. So, when you build a house, first of all you have to have the idea to do it. You have to want to do it. You have to set the intention. I want to build a house. And you have to think about, well, where do I want to build it? What kind of house do I want to build? For how many people, how many bedrooms? How big a house and what do I want to do with that house? Do I want to entertain or do I want something simple to take care of. So all creations starts with thought, it starts with an idea. And we get lots of ideas in the course of our life and we kind of file them away like an arrow that we put in our back in a quiver. And we say, yeah, someday I'd like to do that. I have lots of ideas for books I want to write and I go yeah, someday I'll write a book about that. But when you begin to take the downward current, you say, all right, today I'm going to pull that arrow out of my quiver and I'm going to set an intention. Now I'm going to build, begin building this house or now I'm going to write this book. Or now I'm going to make this for dinner. It could be as simple as that. Or now I'm going to take that vacation. Now, you're notching up that arrow in your quiver and you're aiming it toward your goal. So setting intention and having the idea is seventh chakra. And the manifestation principle here is consciousness creates. Everything that comes into creation started with an idea. And then as you continue to think about your idea, you begin to imagine it or maybe even at the same time. You visualize your house. What kind of house do you want it to look like? You visualize your house. What do you want it to look like? What do you want it to look like as you walk in the door? What do you want to see out through the windows? What do you want your kitchen to look like? And in this visualization process you're probably going to be visiting other people's houses and looking at them differently than you would. You're going to look at what they did with their kitchen or different architectural aspects. Maybe you're looking through magazines, pictures of houses or kitchens to get more ideas. This all takes place through the visual frame and that's sixth chakra, the chakra that sees. And so, the manifestation principle here is vision vitalizes. Consciousness creates but vision vitalizes. It's sort of like you can have a line drawing but when you color it in with color it brings it to life. So, once you visualized your house that you want to build and you've gotten clear enough about what you want, you're going to go talk to somebody about it, probably an architect. And you're going to sit down with the architect and you're going to say, well, here's what I want and here's how I envision it, and here's what I've seen in my mind. And the architect's going to ask you questions that's going to take you into further clarification. They're going to say, well, how many square feet do you want the kitchen to be and what is your budget? And what kind of materials do you want? And do you want the windows to face north, east, south or west? How many bedrooms and what kind of carpet? And these are things that make you refine your vision. So, when we communicate, that's fifth chakra, and the manifestation principle here is communication catalyzes. When you talk about your dream, you may find someone else that has an idea, someone else that helps you refine your vision, someone else that gives you feedback and you get more clear and more specific by talking about it. So the realm of relationships is the heart chakra. The principle here is love launches. We want to treat all our relationships with love and respect and positive regard. That's the way you'll get the most out of your relationships. And in any dream that you want to create, there's probably lots of relationships you need to have. In the dream of building a house, you need a relationship with the architect, probably a relationship with the banker to get some money. You need maybe a relationship with a real estate agent that's going to find you the piece of land. You're going to have a relationship with the contractor and all the workers. You're probably going to have to relate to the neighbors and tell them trucks are going to be coming in and building the house. You want the house to relate to the land. So there's lots of relationships you're going to have. And so, when you're looking at your dream it's good to make a list of all those relationships and call them in. Sometimes just naming those relationships help them come into being. For example, after I created my DVD, The Illuminated Chakras, I decided I wanted to put it in some other languages and I wanted Spanish, Italian, French and German. And I want online and I looked at who does translations and voiceovers and everybody was very far away, and I didn't know who was good, and it was very expensive. And so I just set the intention that I would find the right person. Well, two weeks later, I went to a party, kind of a networking party. The first person I met handed me a card and she said she did voiceover translations and I said really. And I said what languages? And she says, "Well, I'm native in French and Italian "and I have a co-worker that does Spanish, "and she knows someone that does German." She named the four languages that I want. And when I told her what the project was, The Illuminated Chakras, she says, "Oh, I've seen that movie. "I would love to do that." She was half the price, she was right there. Within a month I had the whole project done. So now that you've done all these planning and communicating and relating in the upper chakras, now you come to the third chakra. This is the hard part, this is where you have to do something. Third chakra is oriented to action. The manifestation principle here is power produces. So you want to empower yourself to get things done because that's how you're going to produce the results that you need. So, we make a plan. We prioritize our plan. We say, okay, I have to do this first and then I have to do that. You have to build the walls before you can put the roof on and you have to build the foundation before you can build the walls. So, in every project we take into bite size chunks and you say yes, this I can do. If you look at the whole thing all at once it can be overwhelming. But you say okay, in six months I'll get this done. In the next six months I'll get that done. First, I'll write the business plan then I'll find the bankers, then I'll do the project, then I'll build the house. So if you want to attract customers or clients or business people or collaborators, then you want to make it pleasurable and that will keep you on track. And the other aspect of this chakra is once you've started to do this work and you're really taking your action steps and moving things forward, you start to get little results. And then after all these work, we finally come down to the manifested plane, the root chakra. Here the principle is matter matters. And in building a house for example, it really matters that you cut the boards to exactly the right length, that you nail them together in a very specific way, that you have glass for each and every window, that you have enough bricks and cement, and that you follow the plans exactly as they're meant to be. LESSON 36 - Bio-Energetic Movements

- Yesterday we talked about fear being one of the challenges of this chakra. And these exercises these bio-energetic movements and the yoga they're ways to condition the body to run energy through the places that might have become constricted. And as you do, you'll feel safer and more secure. So let's go into some bio-energetic movements for charging and discharging the legs. First one is a standing bio-energetic grounding. So stand upright, your feet hip width apart or even shoulder width the apart I find most people bring their feet too close together. Turn your heels out a little wider than your toes and soften your knees. So you're bending your knee out over your second toe. Ideally you would see your big toenail right on the inside of your knee cap. That is if there's no clothing or anything in the way. And now press down and out with your feet as if you're trying to push apart to floorboards, or you're trying to stretch a sticky mat that you're standing on. And notice how your ground really hooks on. How it really grabs hold, how your base becomes more stable. If someone were going to push you around from this place they'd have a harder time doing it. So that's the grounding stance now to charge it up inhale and bend your knees a little bit more keeping your shoulders over your hips. And as you exhale, push down through the core of each leg push down and out with your feet, and very slowly begin to straighten your knees but don't straighten them all the way maybe 90% of the way. Then inhale and bend again, inhale deeply press those knees down and exhale, press down and out through your legs as if you're pushing the floor away and the result of that is your legs begin to straighten but it's a slow movement. Come to about 90% of the straight don't lock your knees, then inhale again. And go back and forth, inhaling and bending, exhaling pushing through the core of each leg. Now if you're doing this correctly you're going to start to feel a little bit of trembling in your legs, and that's a sign of charge or energy coming up your legs. That's what you want. That's delivering some energy through the roots of your legs, up into your first chakra. Now if that brings up too much charge for you you might want to do a little discharging, that also happens to the legs and feet. So simply run in place and stamp your feet into the ground and let that release, do it until you feel tired and then stand still and feel. You're going to feel calmer in your legs. Maybe a little more expansive. That's what it feels like to discharge. So now that you've gotten a little energy coming in and going out and you've felt what that's like, we're going to take this into a yoga flow. We'll do a little more charging and discharging but we're mostly going to flow into our root chakra. So get ready. Be in clothes you can stretch in get on your mat and follow along with us. What we call the butterfly exercise, will be the charging. And the pelvic pulses that is rocking your pelvis back and forth will be the discharging. Both of these are listed in your workbook. LESSON 36 - Chakra Yoga Flows

- [Instructor] Welcome to your First Chakra Yoga Flow. Before you step on your mat, take a deep breath and let go of all your worries and frustrations, let them drain down into the floor. Step onto your mat with intention, knowing you're stepping into a sacred place, this is the floor of your temple. Place your feet carefully hip-width apart making the outside of your feet parallel to each other. Ground down into your heels, lift up into your crown and extend yourself from Earth to Heaven. Inhale your hands up overhead, and reach higher to the heaven while bending your knees, taking your tailbone behind you and slowly bringing your arms forward, reaching from your tailbone out to your fingertips. Pull your shoulders back, lift the chest, and press down and out with your feet. Inhale and come back up, inhaling your hands up overhead, straightening your legs, reaching once more, And on the exhale, take your arms down around your side, place them on your hips and bend forward all the way keeping your knees bent. And wrapping your arms around your thighs, bringing your belly as close to your thighs as possible, give your legs a hug. On the inhale, press your knees back until you find your edge, then release your hands, take them to the floor. Straighten your legs and inhale halfway up, extending from the tailbone to the crown. Deep breath in and then lower back down, hands on either side of your feet. Once again, honoring your legs that carry you on the journey. And the next breath in, take your right foot back into a High Lunge, straightening the right leg, hugging the muscles to the bone and pressing your left foot into the mat and drawing it toward your right foot. Feel the stability that comes from anchoring into the ground. Take a breath here and slowly lower your right knee down to the floor, flatten your right foot. And gently bend your left leg, sliding your hands back using blocks if necessary. As you straighten your left leg and flex the left foot make some circles with your left ankle clockwise and counterclockwise to exercise the foot and the ankle. And then with toes pointing toward the ceiling and the foot flexed gently press your left heel into the mat, drawing the left leg up into the hip socket as you press your tailbone out behind you, inhale and lengthen through the crown. And on the exhale, keep that length as you slowly bow over your left leg, go to wherever you find your edge. If you need to use blocks, that's fine. If you only touch your knee, that's fine. Press your tailbone out behind you. And then on the next breath in, lift your head, bend your left knee back out over the left foot, tuck your toes behind you, hands on either side of your front foot. Then take your left foot back next to your right for a Downward Dog. On the next breath in, lower your hips, move your shoulders over your hands, bend your knees, take your knees, chest, and chin down to the mat. Wiggle that tailbone a little bit just so you feel it and then lower your hips. And just with the muscles of your back do just a Baby Cobra, lifting your crown, hugging your legs towards each other. And on the exhalation, lower back down, tuck your toes in behind you, press your hands into the floor, press your hips back up once again for a Downward Dog. Stretching into your Dog, wiggling each knee, pressing into the four corners of your mat, anchoring into the ground. On the next breath in, take your right foot up between your hands bending your right knee. And slowly lower down onto your left knee, flattening the left foot. Place your hands on your block or slide them along the floor as you slowly straighten your right leg. Flex your right foot, make some circles with your ankle clockwise and counterclockwise, pointing and flexing the toes. And then with your toes pointed straight up and your foot flexed, press gently into your right heel, hugging the right leg into the hip socket. And lengthen through your tailbone and your crown, inhale. And as you exhale, keep that length as you bring the center of your torso down over your right leg to wherever you find your edge. Just pause at that edge and allow your breath to so gently move you maybe a quarter of an inch with each exhale, without strain pulling the roots down out of the base of the spine. And then on the next breath, inhale your head up and your right knee forward, press the left toes underneath and bring your left foot forward next to your right. And once again, in a Forward Fold let gravity pull your spine down, let your head be heavy, your neck loose, let your legs support you, and feel this hinge at your hips. Softly bend your knees as you rise up, lifting your arms up into a Chair Pose in front of you, pulling the shoulders back, lifting the chest, pressing down into both feet down into the ground and then press through the core of each leg as you slowly come to a stand. Lift your hands up overhead bring your palms together and slide them down the core of your body to your heart. Anchor down into your feet and feel your ground. So now, we want to become anchored like a tree, this is good for developing the strength in your legs and your balance. So, bring your weight onto your right leg, maybe just gently touching your left toes to give you balance. And anchor down through that right leg, all the way from the crown of your head to the heel of your foot. And staying in balance, slowly lift your left foot and place it either against your right ankle for a beginner pose, or you can move it higher up and place the foot against your thigh, and take the left knee out to the side. And if you're in good balance, you can take your hands up and then bring them back down to the heart and slowly lower your left foot. Shake your legs out, and now place your weight on your left foot. Gently lift your right foot so your toes are touching as you establish your balance, grounding down through the root of your left leg. And when you feel that balance in your core, take your right foot against your right ankle or higher up, depending on your flexibility, and bring your hands together over your heart. Feel the trunk of your tree anchored down into the roots of your left leg as you lift your crown, tuck your tailbone. And if you're in good balance, you can lift your hands up overhead, expanding your branches. Take a breath in and bring your hands back over your heart, and bring your right foot down again. Shake your legs out and feel your ground. Now, that both feet are on the ground, stand and feel your legs as roots supporting your body. LESSON 36 - Everyday Movements

- So in each chakra we're going to learn some everyday movement, simple things you can do in a matter of seconds to begin to develop new habits in your body to open your chakras. So in the first chakra, one of them is to create a wide base. And we do that by taking the tailbone which we know curls under in the spine and energetically pressing it toward the back of your seat. So anytime you sit down to a meal, to work at your computer, to sit in the driver's seat and drive a car, to have a conversation with someone, just simply take your tailbone back and notice how that begins to set the tone to have an upright spine. And one more thing you can do that's really fun is to just bounce up and down on your tailbone. You can do it on the floor and move side to side. You can do it on a chair. And what that does, it stimulates the base of the spine and starts the cerebral spinal fluid moving up and down. It's fun and it helps you remember your first chakra. Remember, anytime you lose your first chakra, just sit down. That's where it is. You're sitting on it. Some everyday movements that you can do that just take a matter of seconds? Well, as you stand, as you inhale take your tailbone way back. Arch the small of your back a little bit. As you exhale, swing it forward. Just practice breathing in and out, swinging your pelvis backwards and forward. Once you get the hang of moving it backward and forward, you can now move it forward and let a wave form go all the way up your body. So inhale, take it back. Exhale, take your pelvis forward and let that movement make a wave motion all the way up to your crown. So one of the everyday movements you can do is to work with the breath. This comes from yoga called the breath of fire, or Kapalbhati, and it's a rapid diaphragmatic breathing. Just take your hand and place it over your solar plexus, over your third chakra. Relax your breath. Just let the breath come in naturally. And then snap your diaphragm back toward your spine and send the air out through your nose like that. Then when you relax your diaphragm the air naturally comes back in and when you snap it, it comes out again. So do that rapidly like this. And just notice, do you feel a little bit more energy? This is also good for toning the muscles in front of the third chakra. Another charging breath that you can do, especially if you get a little stiff in the middle, is inhale your belly to the front and take it around the back and stir the cauldron. Keep your shoulders over your hips and just try to move this midsection of your body. When you get the hang of it one way, go around the other way, inhaling when it's front, exhaling to the back. And then as you pause, stop and see, do you feel a little activation in your third chakra? You can use these exercises when you need a little more containment for your power. That's the breath of fire, or a little bit of development of that muscle that holds your third chakra in place, or when you just want to loosen things up and activate your third chakra, maybe you want to stimulate your metabolism or wake yourself up, stir that cauldron and see what happens. One is just to open your hands up, take your shoulders back in a kind of "ain't it wonderful" feeling. So that just lifts the heart. Just look around at any kind of magic or miracle you see around you and just "ah, ain't it wonderful". Feel how that opens your heart. And the other one is very simple, several times in your day, especially when you're busy or hurrying somewhere, just take a moment to stop, take a deep breath into your heart and lift the corners of your mouth toward your ears. So one is when your neck gets tired, especially you've been sitting at your computer for awhile. Just kind of take your head and roll it around, stretching the neck on each part. If you go to one side, you might take the opposite hand and pull your ear down towards your shoulder a little. The free hand can then massage some of the muscles on your neck. You can take it to the back and you can take the other side, do a little massaging up and down. And that helps to relieve some neck tension. Shake your head side to side and just loosen it up. Another one to work with the tension that happens in the jaw from clenching your jaw and closing your throat chakra is that if you take your hand, or even someone else can do this to you, and put it under your chin and then open your mouth and make a sound. So you're pressing against the resistance of your hand. Ah! And that means your jaw muscles have to go the other way and open. And that's a good way to release jaw tension. So there's an eye exercise that comes from yoga that is good for strengthening the muscles of your eyes. And actually they say it is good for helping to improve your vision. And it's simply looking in different directions systematically. Yogic eye exercises. Look directly forward from a calm place, and then following a straight line, lift your eyes up, looking as high as you can without moving your head, looking up toward your eyebrows, and then a straight line down past the center line and look down below again without moving your head. Then bring your eyes once more up to center. And now, without moving your head, take your eyes to the right, as far as you can, and then looking across a horizontal line, take them to the left as far as you can, and back to center. Now we're going to go diagonally. Looking to the upper right across the center and to the lower left, again without moving your head, and back to center. And now up to the upper left and down to the lower right, and back to center. Now we're going to lift our eyes up again without moving the head and take them around the clock to the right, down below up the left, circle them around a couple of times and then back to center. And then once again, lift your eyes upward without moving your head, take them around the clock in the opposite direction to the left and down and to the right and up couple of times, and then back to center. Then close your eyes and rub your hands together creating some friction and some heat in your palms. And when you feel that heat in your palms, gently cup your hands over your eyes and feel the warmth. So I mentioned how, when we block off this chakra we often furrow our brow. So a nice thing to do is do a forehead pull. Take your forefingers along the midline of your forehead and press in and pull out toward the side of your head, maybe a couple times. And then when you get to your temples, massage your temples and then back to the inner corner of your eyebrows really press is probably going to be a little tender, and pull, follow your eyebrows out, just massaging gently. And then I like to take it around to the bottom of the skull and just do a little tapping here. That's a good third eye stimulation.

LESSON 36 - Meditation: Chakra Alignment Meditation: Opening Inner Temple

- Opening the inner temple. Chakra alignment meditation. Find it quiet place where you can sit comfortably. Make this a special time for yourself. Time to go inside to your inner temple, that sacred space within your skin, that you identify as yourself. Let the images of the day fall away as your attention turns inward, into the peaceful sanctuary of your inner world. Begin to focus on your breath, naturally coming in and coming out. Letting the inhalation be just a little bigger and then letting it out all the way, even with a soft sigh. Wait for the natural inclination to inhale again and imagine the air streaming into your inner temple like a fresh breeze through a window. And release again, releasing any tension in your body and settling in to the depth of your soul. Say hello to this inner temple. Take up residence here, this is your sacred space Yours and yours alone. Begin to align your chakras by pressing your tailbone toward the back of your seat, widening your base. Notice what happens to your body, to your posture, to your breath. From the center of that wide base, press down into the earth, pressing down through any floors or foundations, to imagine strong and vital roots penetrating the earth below. Feel the sense of settling into the floor of your inner temple, into your foundation of being, into the home of your body. Now, keeping your roots down, lift the top of your head up toward the heavens, inhale into the vast spaciousness of the starry night sky and feel yourself expand into the infinite. Imagine you can lift higher and higher, yet still keep your roots anchored in the earth. Extending upward and downward at the same time. Filling your spine. When you come to your next exhalation, draw that cosmic energy downward into the crown of your head. And down through the core that runs through the vertical center of your temple. See that core in your mind's eye as a vertical column of sparkling, bright energy. Imagine that column of energy as the capital letter I. A straight line with a little hat at the top and a foot at the bottom. Feel that core as your personal eye, the sacred center of your inner temple. As you breathe in silently utter the word I and affirm that core, bringing in beautiful golden energy from your crown. And as you breathe out, imagine the words I am, moving the energy all the way down to the earth Affirm the I on the in breath, and the I am on the out breath. I on the in breath and I am on the out breath. And then feeling that I, the presence that is you. Now give it a location. I am here, I am in here. I am here now. Now that you have established your core, imagine that strong like spinning, shining jewels, along the cord of your central column of energy are the seven chakras, seven chambers in your inner temple. Each one handling a different type of energy. We will now charge up each one of these sacred chambers with the breath. Beginning at the base of the spine, where the first chakra is located. Imagine a red, glowing ball of energy. Roots moving down to the earth, pushing into the solid body of the mother. Inhale and draw that earth energy up your legs and into your body and exhale and push it back down to the earth. Pressing your tailbone to the back, your sitting bones down, your feet into the floor. Say, I am in in here. Inhale and draw the earth energy up the way roots drop nutrients and exhale and let your roots penetrate even deeper. One more time, inhaling up exhaling, pressing the roots deep and wide. All the way around you, like the roots of a tree. And on the next breath, bring your attention to your second chakra. Just below the navel, midway between front and back. Its name, svadhisthana, means ones own place. So acknowledge this as your private place, an intimate place. The chakra of water who's flow is the river of life, flowing through you moment to moment. Allow those rivers to flow through your body right now, making little micro movements wherever you're sitting, oscillating back and forth with your spine according to what feels good to you. Imagine a warm orange color expanding out to your skin as you inhale. And then with a sensuous caress, draw that energy in to your own place. Inhale and and expand into the orange, exhale and gather that light into your core. Seeing the light brighten right in the center of your inner place. Imagine this center directly above the red first chakra, in alignment, the radiant core connecting them. And as that radiant core moves through the second chakra, it rises up into the fire of the third chakra. Here, the energy of matter and movement combine to create friction and sparks energy. That energy can bring you power. Imagine that fire burning inside you, burning with purpose, burning with strength, feel the energy of that fire. Feel that charge to go forth and take action, to do what needs to be done. As you inhale, imagine the yellow fire expanding. And as you exhale, draw those flames into embers, knowing you can breathe in those sparks any time and move it into a fire, and you can let go of the breath and come into a calm. And now your red first chakra, your orange second chakra, your golden yellow third chakra connected along the radiant core which now rises out of that fire. Up into the air of the heart. Take a breath of this glorious air, fill yourself with its presence and let it out. Softening the body is your release. Let the next breath in be breathing in the love that brings everything in this world into relationship. The love that has provided this earth and all the beings on it. And as you breathe out, let that love flow through your heart. Loving creation in return, in gratitude, inhaling the love in like a divine caress to your heart, filling your heart with beautiful green energy and then releasing. Opening the chest, softening the shoulders, opening the arms wide. Maybe you would like to bring your hands over your own heart, holding this precious jewel, this sacred center of the heart chakra. Anahata, sound that is made without any two things striking. And as the heart settles into the peace, the unity and expansion of the air. We spread our wings and fly up to the throat chakra. The realm of sound, vibration, the bright blue of communication, expression, creativity. Allow the music to be a caress to your fifth chakra. See waves of radiant blue light, oscillating sound waves moving out from your throat and moving inward to your inner listening. Imagining your expression to be effortless. Your deepest truth abides here. As the vibrations of this sound massage your being, imagine rising to even a higher, faster vibration of light. The light of the sixth chakra, the place of vision, intuition, imagination. Now we feel the charge of our life force is a luminous light that comes pouring in from the sunlight, pouring in like light through a window and illuminating the inner temple. Cascading down through the center, where we see these beautiful, colored jewels spinning and sparkling, strung together by the luminous, radiant core. And as you breathe in, imagine this light expands. And floods your being. And as you breathe out, imagine you focus that light into a laser beam, penetrating focus to see forward, to shine a light on whatever you need to see. And inhaling and expanding into the light, exhaling and focusing, what is yours to do? What is your vision? What is your dream? We finally take the last step up to the crown chakra. Sahasrara, 1000 petal lotus, fully blooming at the crown of the head, consciousness itself. Who is it that is hearing these words? Who is it that is hearing this music, that is living in your body, who's lives in this sacred temple? The answer to this is the same as what is asking, consciousness itself. But it is not you alone that is conscious, but everything around you. Open to the divine cosmos the way a flower drinks in the sunlight, pulling it down, letting it tumble into your inner temple, filling each chakra overflowing to the one below. Radiant nectar of the gods caressing you with divine intelligence, guidance, wisdom. Let this wisdom settle within you and from your mind's eye, see this radiant inner temple, seven rainbow jewels spinning on a radiant core. The core of the eye, the core of the south. These radiant jewels shining out into the world around you. Radiating love and light and truth power, pleasure. The infinite presence of your being. Know that this is what you are, a rainbow bridge from heaven to earth, complete and whole and present.

LESSON 36 - Meditation: Chakra Healing: Harvesting Your Day Meditation

- Harvesting your day into your chakras, a meditation to aid you in falling asleep. As your day winds into a close, and you climb into your bed at night, know that you are pulling into yourself to drop down and to go to sleep. Align your body vertically on your back and close your eyes. Sink into the softness of the bed, and feel that your day is ending. Harvest memories through each chakra that you can pull into your inner temple and keep. We begin at the crown, a chakra of consciousness and awareness, spirituality. What was the spiritual moment that you had today? Perhaps a moment of realization or awakening? An insight? Maybe a good meditation? Take a moment to review that experience. Draw it into your crown chakra. And like a flower folding up for the night, fold up the thousand petals of the crown chakra lotus. And take that memory inside, and let it settle. Take a breath in and experience a moment of gratitude for what you just harvested. And next, come down to your sixth chakra, the chakra of seeing. What did you see today that was beautiful? Do you remember color or light? A smile on a child's face? A beautiful person walking down the street? A landscape? And if nothing comes to mind, you can always create something in your imagination, something of beauty, to harvest into the core of your sixth chakra. As the two petals of that lotus close like your two eyes, and pull that memory in to the deep Take a breath fully in, and as you let it out, let that settle down into your body. And next, review the conversations you had today. Was there a moment when you felt particularly connected? Where you spoke your truth or heard someone else's truth? Or a moment of hearing beautiful music? Gather this memory into your throat chakra, and fold up the 16 petals of the throat, to keep that memory inside, as you take a deep breath in and out, letting that settle deep into your core. Next, bring your attention to your heart chakra, in the middle of your chest. Where did you love today? Where did you receive love? Where did you give love? Where did you do something that you love? A moment when your heart soared? Fold up the 12 petals of your heart chakra lotus and bring it inside to your inner temple. Take a breath in and let it out. And let that love settle in the deepest part of your being. Now, move your attention down to your third chakra in the solar plexus, the power center. Where did you feel powerful today? What was a moment when you had a lot of energy? When you were strong and effective? What did it feel like to have that power coursing through your veins? Fold up the 10 petals of the third chakra, and bring that power into your core and let it settle. And now, you come down to your second chakra, the center of pleasure. How did you feel today? What did you do that was pleasurable, enjoyable, fun? Do you remember laughing or playing? Or perhaps it was a touch on your skin? A delicious taste at a meal? A way your body moved? Harvest that feeling of pleasure into the cells of your body, as you breathe in to your second chakra. Folding up the six petals of the second chakra lotus and letting that pleasure settle in your body for the night. And then finally, as you settle down into your body, to thank your body for what it went through today. Thank your body for doing the work that you did. Reviewing what touched your body. What did you eat? Where did you go? And feel gratitude for another day of living. All these experiences folding up the petals, bringing it inside and letting it settle in the deep core of your being. And as your breath softens and the day drifts away, know that these treasures are yours to keep as you drift off to a deep and restful sleep.
